Each province and region boasts its own beauty. For example, when we talk about Ninh Binh, we can't forget the Trang An-Bai Dinh tourist complex. And when we mention Phan Thiet in Binh Thuan, we can't leave out the eco-tourism destination of Bau Trang Mui Ne.\n\nMui Ne is one of the most picturesque and serene coastal eco-tourism destinations in Binh Thuan province. Visitors to Mui Ne are captivated not only by the pristine natural beauty but also by modern water sports, outdoor adventures, and the local way of life. The endless sandy beaches, perfect for swimming in the warm waters or sunbathing, are a paradise for those who want to relax under the shade of tall coconut trees, enjoying the refreshing sea breeze.\n\nKey Features of Mui Ne:\n\nMui Ne is a famous tourist destination in Phan Thiet known for its long stretches of white sand, azure seas, and swaying coconut trees. The harmony of golden sands, radiant sunshine, and deep blue sea creates a warm and inviting atmosphere that attracts numerous travelers.\n\nNotable Attractions in Mui Ne:\n\nTruong Duc Thanh - Ho Chi Minh Museum: This school was founded by patriotic scholars in 1907 to support the Duy Tan movement in Central Vietnam. Truong Duc Thanh also holds historical significance as President Ho Chi Minh taught here in 1910 before he went to Saigon to seek ways to save the nation.\n\nHo Chi Minh Museum (Binh Thuan Branch): Located within the Truong Duc Thanh compound in Phan Thiet city, this museum was established on May 19, 1986. It preserves nearly all of the belongings of teacher Nguyen Tat Thanh (Ho Chi Minh) from nearly a century ago.\n\nDinh Van Thuy Tu Temple: Situated in the Ng\u01b0 \u00d4ng area of \u0110\u1ee9c Th\u1eafng Ward in Phan Thiet, this temple worships Nam Hai deity, also known as Ca \u00d4ng (whale). The temple houses the skeleton of a giant Ca \u00d4ng whale, weighing 65 tons and measuring 22 meters in length, making it the largest in Vietnam and Southeast Asia. Annual ceremonies are held on various lunar calendar dates to honor the whale, featuring activities like traditional opera, boat racing, and more.\n\nLau Ong Hoang: Along the Mui Ne tourism road, you'll find Lau Ong Hoang, a place associated with the famous poet Han Mac Tu. Lau Ong Hoang was a rendezvous point for Han Mac Tu and Mong Cam, the poet's lover. Han Mac Tu wrote many poems about the picturesque scenery of this place.\n\nPoshanu Tower: Located on Ba Nai Hill in Phu Hai Ward, about 7 km northeast of Phan Thiet's city center, the Cham Poshanu Tower is a well-preserved relic of the ancient Champa Kingdom. It exhibits the H\u00f2a Lai architectural style, one of Champa's ancient art styles. Despite its relatively small size, it showcases the architectural and artistic excellence of ancient Champa. Poshanu Tower is named after Princess Poshanu, a beloved figure in Cham culture.\n\nBai Rang (Rang Beach): This is the most beautiful beach in Phan Thiet, located about 15 km north of the city center, surrounded by dense coconut groves resembling a beautiful coconut forest. During the summer, Rang Beach is bustling with beachgoers enjoying the warm waters and savoring delicious grilled green fish.\n\nHon Rom (Rom Island): Less than 1 km from Mui Ne, Hon Rom, also known as Hon Lao, remains relatively untouched. You can reach it by taking a boat ride offered by hotels or hiring a fishing boat for a round trip. Hon Rom features crystal-clear waters, visible coral reefs, and large rock formations. The best time to visit is in the evening, as you'll witness the beauty of the sunset and twilight over the sea.\n\nDoi Cat Bay (White Sand Dunes): Near Hon Rom, one of the most enchanting sights that once mesmerized poets, painters, and photographers is the Mui Ne sand dunes (located in Ward 5, Mui Ne). Besides their beautiful shape, the sands here come in various colors, with up to 18 different shades. Visitors can rent a board for sandboarding and afterward enjoy coconut water and Banh Bot Loc, a local delicacy.\n\nBau Trang - Bau Sen: Located 18 km from Hon Rom, these are two natural freshwater lakes amidst the vast white sand dunes. Bau Trang, also known as Bau Ong, is famous for its lotus flowers blooming among the white sand dunes during the summer. On the other hand, Bau Sen, also known as Bau Ba, is a large, pristine lake surrounded by beautiful and pure sand dunes.\n\nDoi Cat Trang (White Sand Hills): Also known as Doi Cat Bau Trang, these sand dunes encompass the large Bau Sen lake. They are often referred to as the Sahara Desert of Vietnam due to their pure white sands and stunning surrounding landscapes. This destination is a must-visit when traveling to Phan Thiet, Binh Thuan.\n\nSuoi Tien (Fairy Stream): This destination is often affectionately named the \"Land of Fairy Tales.\" Suoi Tien in Mui Ne is a small water stream located next to Hon Rom. It's a walking stream with a picturesque sandy valley. You'll also find natural red and white rock formations. Over time, erosion has created unique natural rock formations that make this place fascinating.\n\nMui Ne Fishing Village: Located about 3 km north of Mui Ne town, this village offers an authentic glimpse into the lives of fishermen. As you enter the village, you'll see hundreds of fishing boats of various colors anchored on the water. Nearby, a small market with a serene ambiance is surrounded by coconut trees. Strolling along the beach with seashells scattered everywhere, especially at the boat harbor and the southern part of the town, you can observe how fishermen sort and process their catch.\n\n#Vietnam Join me as I uncover hidden treasures, share travel tips, and embrace diverse", "created": "2023-08-17 10:51:25+00:00", "followersCount": 1178, "friendsCount": 939, "statusesCount": 4252, "favouritesCount": 5336, "listedCount": 0, "mediaCount": 211, "location": "", "profileImageUrl": "https://pbs.twimg.com/profile_images/1692127431195611136/_shmj8fw_normal.jpg", "profileBannerUrl": "https://pbs.twimg.com/profile_banners/1692126822195171328/1692276362", "protected": null, "verified": false, "blue": true, "blueType": null, "descriptionLinks": [], "_type": "snscrape.modules.twitter.User"}, "lang": "en", "rawContent": "Vietnam, our country, stretches from the North to the South, and everywhere you go, you'll find breathtaking natural landscapes and unique cultural heritage that leave people in awe. Each province and region boasts its own beauty. For example, when we talk about Ninh Binh, we can't forget the Trang An-Bai Dinh tourist complex. And when we mention Phan Thiet in Binh Thuan, we can't leave out the eco-tourism destination of Bau Trang Mui Ne.\n\nMui Ne is one of the most picturesque and serene coastal eco-tourism destinations in Binh Thuan province. Visitors to Mui Ne are captivated not only by the pristine natural beauty but also by modern water sports, outdoor adventures, and the local way of life. The endless sandy beaches, perfect for swimming in the warm waters or sunbathing, are a paradise for those who want to relax under the shade of tall coconut trees, enjoying the refreshing sea breeze.\n\nKey Features of Mui Ne:\n\nMui Ne is a famous tourist destination in Phan Thiet known for its long stretches of white sand, azure seas, and swaying coconut trees. The harmony of golden sands, radiant sunshine, and deep blue sea creates a warm and inviting atmosphere that attracts numerous travelers.\n\nNotable Attractions in Mui Ne:\n\nTruong Duc Thanh - Ho Chi Minh Museum: This school was founded by patriotic scholars in 1907 to support the Duy Tan movement in Central Vietnam. Truong Duc Thanh also holds historical significance as President Ho Chi Minh taught here in 1910 before he went to Saigon to seek ways to save the nation.\n\nHo Chi Minh Museum (Binh Thuan Branch): Located within the Truong Duc Thanh compound in Phan Thiet city, this museum was established on May 19, 1986. It preserves nearly all of the belongings of teacher Nguyen Tat Thanh (Ho Chi Minh) from nearly a century ago.\n\nDinh Van Thuy Tu Temple: Situated in the Ng\u01b0 \u00d4ng area of \u0110\u1ee9c Th\u1eafng Ward in Phan Thiet, this temple worships Nam Hai deity, also known as Ca \u00d4ng (whale). The temple houses the skeleton of a giant Ca \u00d4ng whale, weighing 65 tons and measuring 22 meters in length, making it the largest in Vietnam and Southeast Asia. Annual ceremonies are held on various lunar calendar dates to honor the whale, featuring activities like traditional opera, boat racing, and more.\n\nLau Ong Hoang: Along the Mui Ne tourism road, you'll find Lau Ong Hoang, a place associated with the famous poet Han Mac Tu. Lau Ong Hoang was a rendezvous point for Han Mac Tu and Mong Cam, the poet's lover. Han Mac Tu wrote many poems about the picturesque scenery of this place.\n\nPoshanu Tower: Located on Ba Nai Hill in Phu Hai Ward, about 7 km northeast of Phan Thiet's city center, the Cham Poshanu Tower is a well-preserved relic of the ancient Champa Kingdom. It exhibits the H\u00f2a Lai architectural style, one of Champa's ancient art styles. Despite its relatively small size, it showcases the architectural and artistic excellence of ancient Champa. Poshanu Tower is named after Princess Poshanu, a beloved figure in Cham culture.\n\nBai Rang (Rang Beach): This is the most beautiful beach in Phan Thiet, located about 15 km north of the city center, surrounded by dense coconut groves resembling a beautiful coconut forest. During the summer, Rang Beach is bustling with beachgoers enjoying the warm waters and savoring delicious grilled green fish.\n\nHon Rom (Rom Island): Less than 1 km from Mui Ne, Hon Rom, also known as Hon Lao, remains relatively untouched. You can reach it by taking a boat ride offered by hotels or hiring a fishing boat for a round trip. Hon Rom features crystal-clear waters, visible coral reefs, and large rock formations. The best time to visit is in the evening, as you'll witness the beauty of the sunset and twilight over the sea.\n\nDoi Cat Bay (White Sand Dunes): Near Hon Rom, one of the most enchanting sights that once mesmerized poets, painters, and photographers is the Mui Ne sand dunes (located in Ward 5, Mui Ne). Besides their beautiful shape, the sands here come in various colors, with up to 18 different shades. Visitors can rent a board for sandboarding and afterward enjoy coconut water and Banh Bot Loc, a local delicacy.\n\nBau Trang - Bau Sen: Located 18 km from Hon Rom, these are two natural freshwater lakes amidst the vast white sand dunes. Bau Trang, also known as Bau Ong, is famous for its lotus flowers blooming among the white sand dunes during the summer. On the other hand, Bau Sen, also known as Bau Ba, is a large, pristine lake surrounded by beautiful and pure sand dunes.\n\nDoi Cat Trang (White Sand Hills): Also known as Doi Cat Bau Trang, these sand dunes encompass the large Bau Sen lake. They are often referred to as the Sahara Desert of Vietnam due to their pure white sands and stunning surrounding landscapes. This destination is a must-visit when traveling to Phan Thiet, Binh Thuan.\n\nSuoi Tien (Fairy Stream): This destination is often affectionately named the \"Land of Fairy Tales.\" Suoi Tien in Mui Ne is a small water stream located next to Hon Rom. It's a walking stream with a picturesque sandy valley. You'll also find natural red and white rock formations. Over time, erosion has created unique natural rock formations that make this place fascinating.\n\nMui Ne Fishing Village: Located about 3 km north of Mui Ne town, this village offers an authentic glimpse into the lives of fishermen. As you enter the village, you'll see hundreds of fishing boats of various colors anchored on the water. Nearby, a small market with a serene ambiance is surrounded by coconut trees.
